{"id":"FRG-245","title":"Characters cannot overlap — add character-to-character collision","description":"## Problem

Characters walk through each other and stack on the same tile. Pathfinding (A\\*) only avoids walls and furniture. Zero character-to-character collision.

## Technical Assessment (from sub-agent)

**One session. Ship it.** \\~100-200 lines of new/modified code.

### Approach: Dynamic walkable grid + retry + deadlock escape

1. Before each A\\* call, clone the walkable grid and mark other characters' current tiles as unwalkable. Don't reserve destination tiles.
2. On path blocked (A\\* returns no path): wait 500-1000ms, then re-path. The blocker will likely have moved.
3. Deadlock breaker: if re-path fails 3 times, pick a random walkable adjacent tile, move there, then re-path to original goal.
4. Interaction/talk targeting: characters walk to adjacent tile of target. If preferred adjacent tile is blocked, try other adjacent tiles.

### Don't do

* Tile reservation systems
* Movement queues
* Priority-based yielding

### Edge cases to test

* Two characters pathing through each other
* Two characters targeting same object
* Narrow corridor crossing (1-tile wide)
* All adjacent tiles occupied (graceful fallback, not crash)

## Acceptance Criteria

* No two characters occupy the same tile
* Characters path around each other
* No deadlocks (escape valve after 3 retries)

     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting' | 'talking'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→
   152→    // Fallback/re-routing: counts down; engine updates talk route when <= 0
   153→    this._talkRetargetTimer = 0;
   154→
   155→    // Talk targeting — set by AIEngine when walking to meet another character
   156→    this.pendingTalkTarget   = null;  // Character ref awaiting arrival
   157→    this.pendingTalkDialogue = null;  // What A will say when conversation starts
   158→    this.pendingTalkResponse = null;  // What B will say when conversation starts
   159→
   160→    // Active conversation state
   161→    this.talkTimer    = 0;
   162→    this.talkTimerMax = 0;
   163→    this.talkTarget   = null;  // Character ref of current conversation partner
   164→  }
   165→
   166→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   167→
   168→  get px() {
   169→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   170→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   171→    }
   172→    const next = this.path[0];
   173→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   174→  }
   175→
   176→  get py() {
   177→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   178→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   179→    }
   180→    const next = this.path[0];
   181→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   182→  }
   183→
   184→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   185→
   186→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   187→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   188→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   189→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   190→
   191→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   192→      this.path         = path;
   193→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   194→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   195→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   196→      this.action       = 'walking';
   197→
   198→      // Set initial facing from first step
   199→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   200→      this._playWalkAnim();
   201→      return true;
   202→    }
   203→    return false;
   204→  }
   205→
   206→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   207→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs, animType) {
   208→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs, animType);
   209→  }
   210→
   211→  startInteract(target, durationMs, animType) {
   212→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   213→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   214→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   215→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   216→    if (this.sprite) {
   217→      const interactKey = animType ? `${this.name}_interact_${animType}` : null;
   218→      const key = (interactKey && this.sprite.anims.exists(interactKey))
   219→        ? interactKey
   220→        : `${this.name}_idle_anim`;
   221→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   222→    }
   223→  }
   224→
   225→  /** Enter a shared talking state with `partner` for `durationMs` milliseconds. */
   226→  startTalk(partner, durationMs) {
   227→    // Stop any current movement
   228→    this.path        = [];
   229→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   230→
   231→    this.action       = 'talking';
   232→    this.talkTarget   = partner;
   233→    this.talkTimer    = durationMs;
   234→    this.talkTimerMax = durationMs;
   235→
   236→    // Clear any pending object interaction targeting
   237→    this.targetObjectId      = null;
   238→    this.pendingAction       = null;
   239→    // Clear any pending talk targeting (e.g. B was also walking to someone)
   240→    this.pendingTalkTarget   = null;
   241→    this.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   242→    this.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   243→
   244→    if (this.sprite) {
   245→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   246→    }
   247→  }
   248→
   249→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   250→
   251→  update(deltaMs) {
   252→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   253→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   254→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   255→
   256→      // Advance tiles
   257→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   258→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   259→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   260→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   261→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   262→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   263→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   264→      }
   265→
   266→      // Update facing after tile advance so animation matches the current movement direction
   267→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   268→
   269→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   270→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   271→        this.action       = 'idle';
   272→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   273→        this._playAnim('idle');
   274→      } else {
   275→        this._playWalkAnim();
   276→      }
   277→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   278→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   279→      // Ensure idle animation is always playing in idle state (handles external action resets)
   280→      this._playAnim('idle');
   281→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   282→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   283→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   284→        this.action        = 'idle';
   285→        this.interactTarget = null;
   286→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   287→        this._playAnim('idle');
   288→      }
   289→    } else if (this.action === 'talking') {
   290→      this.talkTimer -= deltaMs;
   291→      if (this.talkTimer <= 0) {
   292→        this.action      = 'idle';
   293→        this.talkTarget  = null;
   294→        this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   295→        this._playAnim('idle');
   296→      }
   297→    }
   298→
   299→    // Tick dialogue
   300→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   301→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   302→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   303→    }
   304→
   305→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   306→    if (this.sprite) {
   307→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   308→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   309→    }
   310→
   311→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   312→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   313→    }
   314→  }
   315→
   316→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   317→
   318→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   319→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   320→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   321→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   322→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   323→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   324→    });
   325→  }
   326→
   327→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   328→
   329→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   330→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   331→    const next = this.path[0];
   332→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   333→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   334→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   335→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   336→    } else {
   337→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   338→    }
   339→  }
   340→
   341→  _playAnim(type) {
   342→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   343→    const key = type === 'idle'
   344→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   345→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   346→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   347→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   348→    }
   349→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   350→  }
   351→
   352→  _playWalkAnim() {
   353→    this._playAnim('walk');
   354→  }
   355→}

     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).

     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    56→      });
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    60→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    61→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    62→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    66→      // Defensive release: if interactTarget is set but the character is no longer
    67→      // interacting, an external change (e.g. a stale async AI decision resolving
    68→      // between frames) moved them out of 'interacting' without triggering the
    69→      // normal detection below.  Release the slot now so the object doesn't stay
    70→      // permanently full.
    71→      if (char.interactTarget && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    72→        console.warn(
    73→          `[Engine] defensive release: ${char.name} has interactTarget ` +
    74→          `'${char.interactTarget}' but action='${char.action}' — releasing slot`
    75→        );
    76→        this.objectEngine.release(char.interactTarget, char.name);
    77→        char.interactTarget = null;
    78→      }
    79→
    80→      // Save pre-update state to detect interaction-end transitions
    81→      const prevAction         = char.action;
    82→      const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget;
    83→
    84→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    85→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    86→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    87→      }
    88→
    89→      // Handle arrival: character reached talk target
    90→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {
    91→        this._handleTalkArrival(char);
    92→      }
    93→
    94→      // Mid-walk: periodically re-route toward a moving talk target
    95→      if (char.action === 'walking' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {
    96→        char._talkRetargetTimer -= deltaMs;
    97→        if (char._talkRetargetTimer <= 0) {
    98→          char._talkRetargetTimer = 2000; // re-check every 2 s
    99→          this._updateTalkRoute(char);
   100→        }
   101→      }
   102→
   103→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
   104→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
   105→        this._doWander(char);
   106→      }
   107→
   108→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
   109→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
   110→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
   111→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
   112→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
   113→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
   114→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
   115→        }
   116→      }
   117→
   118→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
   119→      char.update(deltaMs);
   120→
   121→      // Detect interaction end: release slot so other characters can use the object
   122→      if (prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget) {
   123→        this.objectEngine.release(prevInteractTarget, char.name);
   124→      }
   125→    }
   126→  }
   127→
   128→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   129→
   130→  /**
   131→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
   132→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
   133→   * If the object has no valid transition, finds an alternative instead of idling.
   134→   */
   135→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
   136→    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;
   137→    const action   = char.pendingAction || 'use';
   138→
   139→    // Clear targeting immediately so we don't re-fire on the next idle frame.
   140→    // _fallbackToAlternativeObject may set a new targetObjectId if it finds one.
   141→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   142→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   143→
   144→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   145→
   146→    if (event) {
   147→      // Convert reservation → active occupancy
   148→      this.objectEngine.arrive(objectId, char.name);
   149→
   150→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   151→
   152→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   153→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   154→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   155→      if (obj && event.state) {
   156→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   157→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   158→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   159→        }
   160→      }
   161→
   162→      // Face toward the object tile before entering interaction
   163→      if (obj) {
   164→        const dx = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   165→        const dy = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   166→        if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   167→          char.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   168→        } else {
   169→          char.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   170→        }
   171→      }
   172→
   173→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs, obj?.interactAnim ?? null);
   174→
   175→      if (event.speech) char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   176→      if (event.emoji)  this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   177→    } else {
   178→      // No valid transition (object changed state mid-walk) — release the
   179→      // reservation and try to find an alternative object.
   180→      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);
   181→      this._fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, objectId);
   182→    }
   183→  }
   184→
   185→  // ── Talk handshake ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   186→
   187→  /**
   188→   * Called when a character arrives at the tile adjacent to their talk target.
   189→   * Checks proximity and re-evaluates B's availability before starting conversation.
   190→   */
   191→  _handleTalkArrival(char) {
   192→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   193→    char.pendingTalkTarget = null;
   194→
   195→    // Proximity check: target may have moved significantly during the walk.
   196→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   197→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   198→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   199→
   200→    if (dist > 3) {
   201→      // Target has drifted — try to follow if not too far
   202→      if (dist <= 10) {
   203→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   204→        if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   205→          // Re-attach pending talk so we retry on next arrival
   206→          char.pendingTalkTarget   = target;
   207→          char._talkRetargetTimer  = 2000;
   208→          return;
   209→        }
   210→      }
   211→      // Too far or unreachable — abort
   212→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   213→        type:      'fallback',
   214→        charLabel: char.label,
   215→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   216→        fromLabel: target.label,
   217→        toLabel:   null,
   218→      });
   219→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   220→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   221→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   222→      return;
   223→    }
   224→
   225→    // Re-check availability: accept if idle or walking, reject if busy
   226→    const canTalk = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';
   227→
   228→    if (!canTalk) {
   229→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   230→        type:           'talk_rejected',
   231→        initiatorLabel: char.label,
   232→        targetLabel:    target.label,
   233→      });
   234→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   235→      return;
   236→    }
   237→
   238→    this._startConversation(char, target);
   239→  }
   240→
   241→  /**
   242→   * Configurable conversation duration range (ms).
   243→   * Defaults to 10–15 s; override via constructor config.
   244→   */
   245→  get _talkDurationMs() {
   246→    return 10_000 + Math.random() * 5_000;
   247→  }
   248→
   249→  /**
   250→   * Synchronise charA and charB into a shared 'talking' state.
   251→   * Both face each other, AI timers are paused (via action check in AIEngine),
   252→   * and conversation ends naturally when the timer expires.
   253→   */
   254→  _startConversation(charA, charB) {
   255→    // Release any pending object reservation charB held while walking.
   256→    // startTalk() clears targetObjectId without calling objectEngine.release(),
   257→    // so we must do it here before the slot becomes permanently orphaned.
   258→    if (charB.targetObjectId) {
   259→      this.objectEngine.release(charB.targetObjectId, charB.name);
   260→      charB.targetObjectId = null;
   261→      charB.pendingAction  = null;
   262→    }
   263→
   264→    const duration = this._talkDurationMs;
   265→
   266→    // Face each other
   267→    const dx = Math.round(charB.tx) - Math.round(charA.tx);
   268→    const dy = Math.round(charB.ty) - Math.round(charA.ty);
   269→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   270→      charA.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   271→      charB.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'left'  : 'right';
   272→    } else {
   273→      charA.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   274→      charB.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'up'   : 'down';
   275→    }
   276→
   277→    // Transfer queued dialogue to speech bubbles
   278→    if (charA.pendingTalkDialogue) {
   279→      charA.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkDialogue;
   280→      charA.pendingTalkDialogue    = null;
   281→    }
   282→    if (charA.pendingTalkResponse) {
   283→      charB.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkResponse;
   284→      charA.pendingTalkResponse    = null;
   285→    }
   286→
   287→    charA.startTalk(charB, duration);
   288→    charB.startTalk(charA, duration);
   289→
   290→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   291→      type:           'conversation_start',
   292→      initiatorLabel: charA.label,
   293→      targetLabel:    charB.label,
   294→    });
   295→  }
   296→
   297→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   298→
   299→  _doWander(char) {
   300→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   301→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   302→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   303→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   304→        // Shuffle and try each until one has an available slot and a reachable adjacent tile
   305→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   306→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   307→          if (obj.isFull()) continue; // skip objects at capacity
   308→          // Only target objects whose current state accepts a 'use' interaction
   309→          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   310→          if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;
   311→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   312→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   313→            obj.reserve(char.name); // claim a slot before walking
   314→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   315→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   316→            return;
   317→          }
   318→        }
   319→        // All objects full/non-interactable/unreachable — fall through to random wander
   320→      }
   321→    }
   322→
   323→    // Random walkable tile
   324→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   325→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   326→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   327→      return;
   328→    }
   329→
   330→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   331→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   332→
   333→    let moved = false;
   334→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   335→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   336→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   337→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   338→      if (moved) break;
   339→    }
   340→
   341→    if (!moved) {
   342→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   343→    }
   344→  }
   345→
   346→  // ── Fallback helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   347→
   348→  /**
   349→   * Find the closest available object that `char` can interact with right now,
   350→   * excluding the object with `excludeId`.
   351→   * @returns {ObjectInstance|null}
   352→   */
   353→  _findAlternativeObject(char, excludeId) {
   354→    const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   355→    let best     = null;
   356→    let bestDist = Infinity;
   357→
   358→    for (const obj of objects) {
   359→      if (obj.id === excludeId) continue;
   360→      if (obj.isFull()) continue;
   361→      // Require a usable state right now
   362→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   363→      if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;
   364→      // Require a reachable adjacent tile
   365→      if (!this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty)) continue;
   366→
   367→      const dx   = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   368→      const dy   = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   369→      const dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;
   370→      if (dist < bestDist) { bestDist = dist; best = obj; }
   371→    }
   372→
   373→    return best;
   374→  }
   375→
   376→  /**
   377→   * Called when a character's object interaction fails on arrival.
   378→   * Tries to redirect to the nearest available alternative; emits a 'fallback' event.
   379→   */
   380→  _fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, fromId) {
   381→    const fromObj     = this.objectEngine.getById(fromId);
   382→    const alternative = this._findAlternativeObject(char, fromId);
   383→
   384→    if (alternative) {
   385→      const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(alternative.tx, alternative.ty);
   386→      if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   387→        alternative.reserve(char.name);
   388→        char.targetObjectId = alternative.id;
   389→        char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   390→
   391→        this.pendingEvents.push({
   392→          type:      'fallback',
   393→          charLabel: char.label,
   394→          reason:    'object_unavailable',
   395→          fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,
   396→          toLabel:   alternative.name,
   397→        });
   398→        return;
   399→      }
   400→    }
   401→
   402→    // No usable alternative — idle
   403→    char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   404→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   405→      type:      'fallback',
   406→      charLabel: char.label,
   407→      reason:    'object_unavailable',
   408→      fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,
   409→      toLabel:   null,
   410→    });
   411→  }
   412→
   413→  /**
   414→   * Called periodically while a character is walking toward a talk target.
   415→   * Re-routes the character if the target has moved, or aborts if too far.
   416→   */
   417→  _updateTalkRoute(char) {
   418→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   419→    if (!target) return;
   420→
   421→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   422→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   423→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   424→
   425→    // If target has wandered more than 10 tiles away, give up
   426→    if (dist > 10) {
   427→      char.pendingTalkTarget   = null;
   428→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   429→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   430→      char.path                = [];
   431→      char.action              = 'idle';
   432→      char.wanderTimer         = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   433→
   434→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   435→        type:      'fallback',
   436→        charLabel: char.label,
   437→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   438→        fromLabel: target.label,
   439→        toLabel:   null,
   440→      });
   441→      return;
   442→    }
   443→
   444→    // Re-route only if the path end has drifted more than 1 tile from target
   445→    const pathEnd = char.path[char.path.length - 1];
   446→    if (pathEnd) {
   447→      const edx = pathEnd.tx - Math.round(target.tx);
   448→      const edy = pathEnd.ty - Math.round(target.ty);
   449→      if (Math.sqrt(edx * edx + edy * edy) > 1) {
   450→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   451→        if (adjTile) char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty);
   452→      }
   453→    }
   454→  }
   455→
   456→  /**
   457→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   458→   */
   459→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   460→    const dirs = [
   461→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   462→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   463→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   464→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   465→    ];
   466→    for (const d of dirs) {
   467→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   468→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   469→      }
   470→    }
   471→    return null;
   472→  }
   473→
   474→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   475→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   476→    const tiles = [];
   477→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   478→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   479→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   480→      }
   481→    }
   482→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   483→    return tiles;
   484→  }
   485→
   486→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   487→
   488→  getSimTimeString() {
   489→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   490→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   491→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   492→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   493→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   494→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   495→  }
   496→}

     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
    15→ *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
    16→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    17→ *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
    18→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    19→ */
    20→
    21→export class AIEngine {
    22→  /**
    23→   * @param {object}  [config]
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    25→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    26→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    27→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    28→   */
    29→  constructor(config = {}) {
    30→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    31→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    32→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    33→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    34→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    35→
    36→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    37→
    38→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    39→    this._timers = new Map();
    40→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    41→    this._pending = new Set();
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    47→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    48→
    49→    for (const char of characters) {
    50→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    51→      t -= deltaMs;
    52→
    53→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object or in conversation;
    54→      // let the timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    55→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting' && char.action !== 'talking') {
    56→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    57→        this._requestDecision(char, characters, objects, simState);
    58→      } else {
    59→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    60→      }
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→  async _requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState) {
    67→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    68→
    69→    try {
    70→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    71→        .filter(obj => {
    72→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    73→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    74→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    75→        })
    76→        .map(o => {
    77→          const slot = o.getSlotInfo();
    78→          // Resolve reserved/occupied character names → display labels for LLM context
    79→          const reservedBy = (o.getReservations?.() ?? [])
    80→            .map(n => characters.find(c => c.name === n)?.label ?? n);
    81→          const occupiedBy = (o.getOccupants?.() ?? [])
    82→            .map(n => characters.find(c => c.name === n)?.label ?? n);
    83→          return {
    84→            id:         o.id,
    85→            label:      o.label,
    86→            state:      o.state,
    87→            slots:      `${slot.available}/${slot.capacity} available`,
    88→            available:  slot.available > 0,
    89→            // Blackboard: show who is already heading here or using it
    90→            intendedBy: reservedBy,
    91→            usedBy:     occupiedBy,
    92→          };
    93→        });
    94→
    95→      const nearbyCharacters = characters
    96→        .filter(c => {
    97→          if (c.name === character.name) return false;
    98→          const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    99→          const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
   100→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
   101→        })
   102→        .map(c => ({
   103→          label:   c.label,
   104→          tx:      Math.round(c.tx),
   105→          ty:      Math.round(c.ty),
   106→          action:  c.action,
   107→          canTalk: c.action === 'idle' || c.action === 'walking',
   108→        }));
   109→
   110→      const systemPrompt =
   111→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
   112→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
   113→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
   114→
   115→      const userPrompt =
   116→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
   117→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
   118→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
   119→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
   120→        `Nearby characters: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyCharacters)}. ` +
   121→        `Choose one action:
` +
   122→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   123→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   124→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   125→        `  { "action": "talk",     "targetCharacter": "character_label", "dialogue": "what you say", "targetDialogue": "their response", "description": "..." }
` +
   126→        `IMPORTANT: Only choose "talk" if the target character has canTalk:true. Feel free to talk to any available character, not always the same one.`;
   127→
   128→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
   129→
   130→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
   131→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
   132→      const body = JSON.stringify({
   133→        model: this.model,
   134→        max_tokens: 256,
   135→        system: systemPrompt,
   136→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   137→      });
   138→
   139→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   140→
   141→      if (!res.ok) {
   142→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   143→        return;
   144→      }
   145→
   146→      const data = await res.json();
   147→
   148→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   149→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   150→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   151→              ?? null;
   152→
   153→      if (!text) {
   154→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   155→        return;
   156→      }
   157→
   158→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   159→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState);
   160→    } catch (err) {
   161→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   162→    } finally {
   163→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   164→    }
   165→  }
   166→
   167→  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {
   168→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   169→
   170→    // Discard stale async decisions for characters already in a held state.
   171→    // The interaction/talk will release naturally when the timer expires, and
   172→    // applying a movement decision here would move the character away without
   173→    // releasing the object slot — causing a permanent stale occupancy.
   174→    if (character.action === 'interacting' || character.action === 'talking') {
   175→      return;
   176→    }
   177→
   178→    switch (decision.action) {
   179→      case 'move':
   180→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   181→          // Release any pending object reservation before moving freely
   182→          if (character.targetObjectId) {
   183→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   184→            if (prevObj) {
   185→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   186→              if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   187→                simState.pushEvent({
   188→                  type:      'fallback',
   189→                  charLabel: character.label,
   190→                  reason:    'plan_changed',
   191→                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   192→                  toLabel:   null,
   193→                });
   194→              }
   195→            }
   196→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   197→          }
   198→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   199→        }
   200→        break;
   201→
   202→      case 'interact': {
   203→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   204→        if (obj) {
   205→          // If already heading to a different object, release that reservation first
   206→          let abandonedLabel = null;
   207→          if (character.targetObjectId && character.targetObjectId !== obj.id) {
   208→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   209→            if (prevObj) {
   210→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   211→              abandonedLabel = prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name;
   212→            }
   213→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   214→          }
   215→
   216→          // Only commit if a slot is available and object is currently interactable
   217→          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   218→          if (!obj.isFull() && stateDef?.transitions?.use) {
   219→            // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   220→            const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   221→            if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   222→              if (obj.reserve(character.name)) { // claim slot; guard against any race
   223→                character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   224→                character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   225→                if (abandonedLabel && simState?.pushEvent) {
   226→                  simState.pushEvent({
   227→                    type:      'fallback',
   228→                    charLabel: character.label,
   229→                    reason:    'plan_changed',
   230→                    fromLabel: abandonedLabel,
   231→                    toLabel:   obj.label ?? obj.name,
   232→                  });
   233→                }
   234→              }
   235→            }
   236→          } else if (abandonedLabel && simState?.pushEvent) {
   237→            // New target unavailable — character goes idle after abandoning previous
   238→            simState.pushEvent({
   239→              type:      'fallback',
   240→              charLabel: character.label,
   241→              reason:    'object_unavailable',
   242→              fromLabel: abandonedLabel,
   243→              toLabel:   null,
   244→            });
   245→          }
   246→        }
   247→        break;
   248→      }
   249→
   250→      case 'idle':
   251→        // Release any pending reservation, then stay put for one full decision interval
   252→        if (character.targetObjectId) {
   253→          const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   254→          if (prevObj) {
   255→            prevObj.release(character.name);
   256→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   257→              simState.pushEvent({
   258→                type:      'fallback',
   259→                charLabel: character.label,
   260→                reason:    'plan_changed',
   261→                fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   262→                toLabel:   null,
   263→              });
   264→            }
   265→          }
   266→          character.targetObjectId = null;
   267→        }
   268→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   269→        break;
   270→
   271→      case 'talk': {
   272→        const target = characters.find(c => c.label === decision.targetCharacter);
   273→        if (target) {
   274→          // Evaluate Phase: check if B can accept a conversation request.
   275→          // Accept if idle or walking; reject if interacting, talking, or otherwise busy.
   276→          const canAccept = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';
   277→
   278→          if (!canAccept) {
   279→            // B is busy — log the rejection and let A fall back to idle/wander
   280→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   281→              simState.pushEvent({
   282→                type:           'talk_rejected',
   283→                initiatorLabel: character.label,
   284→                targetLabel:    target.label,
   285→                reason:         target.action,
   286→              });
   287→            }
   288→            // A idles for the normal decision interval (fallback handled by Engine wander)
   289→            character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   290→            break;
   291→          }
   292→
   293→          // Release any previous object reservation before walking to talk
   294→          if (character.targetObjectId) {
   295→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   296→            if (prevObj) {
   297→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   298→              if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   299→                simState.pushEvent({
   300→                  type:      'fallback',
   301→                  charLabel: character.label,
   302→                  reason:    'plan_changed',
   303→                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   304→                  toLabel:   target.label,
   305→                });
   306→              }
   307→            }
   308→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   309→          }
   310→
   311→          // Request Phase: walk A to a tile adjacent to B.
   312→          // Arrival handler in Engine will start the shared talking state.
   313→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   314→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   315→            // Store pending talk so Engine knows what to do on arrival
   316→            character.pendingTalkTarget   = target;
   317→            character.pendingTalkDialogue = decision.dialogue       || null;
   318→            character.pendingTalkResponse = decision.targetDialogue || null;
   319→          }
   320→        }
   321→        break;
   322→      }
   323→    }
   324→
   325→    // For talk actions, dialogue is held until both characters enter talking state.
   326→    if (decision.dialogue && decision.action !== 'talk') {
   327→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   328→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   329→    }
   330→
   331→    if (decision.description) {
   332→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   333→    }
   334→
   335→    if (this.onDecision) {
   336→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   337→    }
   338→  }
   339→}
   340→

{"id":"FRG-245","title":"Characters cannot overlap — add character-to-character collision","description":"## Problem

Characters walk through each other and stack on the same tile. Pathfinding (A\\*) only avoids walls and furniture. Zero character-to-character collision.

## Technical Assessment (from sub-agent)

**One session. Ship it.** \\~100-200 lines of new/modified code.

### Approach: Dynamic walkable grid + retry + deadlock escape

1. Before each A\\* call, clone the walkable grid and mark other characters' current tiles as unwalkable. Don't reserve destination tiles.
2. On path blocked (A\\* returns no path): wait 500-1000ms, then re-path. The blocker will likely have moved.
3. Deadlock breaker: if re-path fails 3 times, pick a random walkable adjacent tile, move there, then re-path to original goal.
4. Interaction/talk targeting: characters walk to adjacent tile of target. If preferred adjacent tile is blocked, try other adjacent tiles.

### Don't do

* Tile reservation systems
* Movement queues
* Priority-based yielding

### Edge cases to test

* Two characters pathing through each other
* Two characters targeting same object
* Narrow corridor crossing (1-tile wide)
* All adjacent tiles occupied (graceful fallback, not crash)

## Acceptance Criteria

* No two characters occupy the same tile
* Characters path around each other

  "old_string": "  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {\n    if (!decision?.action) return;\n\n    // Discard stale async decisions for characters already in a held state.\n    // The interaction/talk will release naturally when the timer expires, and\n    // applying a movement decision here would move the character away without\n    // releasing the object slot \u2014 causing a permanent stale occupancy.\n    if (character.action === 'interacting' || character.action === 'talking') {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    switch (decision.action) {\n      case 'move':\n        if (decision.targetTile) {\n          // Release any pending object reservation before moving freely\n          if (character.targetObjectId) {\n            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);\n            if (prevObj) {\n              prevObj.release(character.name);\n              if (simState?.pushEvent) {\n                simState.pushEvent({\n                  type:      'fallback',\n                  charLabel: character.label,\n                  reason:    'plan_changed',\n                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,\n                  toLabel:   null,\n                });\n              }\n            }\n            character.targetObjectId = null;\n          }\n          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);\n        }\n        break;\n\n      case 'interact': {\n        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);\n        if (obj) {\n          // If already heading to a different object, release that reservation first\n          let abandonedLabel = null;\n          if (character.targetObjectId && character.targetObjectId !== obj.id) {\n            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);\n            if (prevObj) {\n              prevObj.release(character.name);\n              abandonedLabel = prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name;\n            }\n            character.targetObjectId = null;\n          }\n\n          // Only commit if a slot is available and object is currently interactable\n          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];\n          if (!obj.isFull() && stateDef?.transitions?.use) {\n            // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)\n            const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);\n            if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {\n              if (obj.reserve(character.name)) { // claim slot; guard against any race\n                character.targetObjectId = obj.id;\n                character.pendingAction  = 'use';\n                if (abandonedLabel && simState?.pushEvent) {\n                  simState.pushEvent({\n                    type:      'fallback',\n                    charLabel: character.label,\n                    reason:    'plan_changed',\n                    fromLabel: abandonedLabel,\n                    toLabel:   obj.label ?? obj.name,\n                  });\n                }\n              }\n            }\n          } else if (abandonedLabel && simState?.pushEvent) {\n            // New target unavailable \u2014 character goes idle after abandoning previous\n            simState.pushEvent({\n              type:      'fallback',\n              charLabel: character.label,\n              reason:    'object_unavailable',\n              fromLabel: abandonedLabel,\n              toLabel:   null,\n            });\n          }\n        }\n        break;\n      }\n\n      case 'idle':\n        // Release any pending reservation, then stay put for one full decision interval\n        if (character.targetObjectId) {\n          const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);\n          if (prevObj) {\n            prevObj.release(character.name);\n            if (simState?.pushEvent) {\n              simState.pushEvent({\n                type:      'fallback',\n                charLabel: character.label,\n                reason:    'plan_changed',\n                fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,\n                toLabel:   null,\n              });\n            }\n          }\n          character.targetObjectId = null;\n        }\n        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;\n        break;\n\n      case 'talk': {\n        const target = characters.find(c => c.label === decision.targetCharacter);\n        if (target) {\n          // Evaluate Phase: check if B can accept a conversation request.\n          // Accept if idle or walking; reject if interacting, talking, or otherwise busy.\n          const canAccept = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';\n\n          if (!canAccept) {\n            // B is busy \u2014 log the rejection and let A fall back to idle/wander\n            if (simState?.pushEvent) {\n              simState.pushEvent({\n                type:           'talk_rejected',\n                initiatorLabel: character.label,\n                targetLabel:    target.label,\n                reason:         target.action,\n              });\n            }\n            // A idles for the normal decision interval (fallback handled by Engine wander)\n            character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;\n            break;\n          }\n\n          // Release any previous object reservation before walking to talk\n          if (character.targetObjectId) {\n            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);\n            if (prevObj) {\n              prevObj.release(character.name);\n              if (simState?.pushEvent) {\n                simState.pushEvent({\n                  type:      'fallback',\n                  charLabel: character.label,\n                  reason:    'plan_changed',\n                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,\n                  toLabel:   target.label,\n                });\n              }\n            }\n            character.targetObjectId = null;\n          }\n\n          // Request Phase: walk A to a tile adjacent to B.\n          // Arrival handler in Engine will start the shared talking state.\n          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));\n          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {\n            // Store pending talk so Engine knows what to do on arrival\n            character.pendingTalkTarget   = target;\n            character.pendingTalkDialogue = decision.dialogue       || null;\n            character.pendingTalkResponse = decision.targetDialogue || null;\n          }\n        }\n        break;\n      }\n    }",
  "new_string": "  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {\n    if (!decision?.action) return;\n\n    // Discard stale async decisions for characters already in a held state.\n    // The interaction/talk will release naturally when the timer expires, and\n    // applying a movement decision here would move the character away without\n    // releasing the object slot \u2014 causing a permanent stale occupancy.\n    if (character.action === 'interacting' || character.action === 'talking') {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    // Build a walkable grid that avoids other characters' current tiles.\n    // Falls back gracefully if buildDynamicWalkable is not provided (e.g. in tests).\n    const dynWalkable = simState?.buildDynamicWalkable?.(character);\n\n    switch (decision.action) {\n      case 'move':\n        if (decision.targetTile) {\n          // Release any pending object reservation before moving freely\n          if (character.targetObjectId) {\n            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);\n            if (prevObj) {\n              prevObj.release(character.name);\n              if (simState?.pushEvent) {\n                simState.pushEvent({\n                  type:      'fallback',\n                  charLabel: character.label,\n                  reason:    'plan_changed',\n                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,\n                toLabel:   null,\n              });\n            }\n          }\n          character.targetObjectId = null;\n        }\n        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;\n        break;\n\n      case 'talk': {\n        const target = characters.find(c => c.label === decision.targetCharacter);\n        if (target) {\n          // Evaluate Phase: check if B can accept a conversation request.\n          // Accept if idle or walking; reject if interacting, talking, or otherwise busy.\n          const canAccept = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';\n\n          if (!canAccept) {\n            // B is busy \u2014 log the rejection and let A fall back to idle/wander\n            if (simState?.pushEvent) {\n              simState.pushEvent({\n                type:           'talk_rejected',\n                initiatorLabel: character.label,\n                targetLabel:    target.label,\n                reason:         target.action,\n              });\n            }\n            // A idles for the normal decision interval (fallback handled by Engine wander)\n            character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;\n            break;\n          }\n\n          // Release any previous object reservation before walking to talk\n          if (character.targetObjectId) {\n            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);\n            if (prevObj) {\n              prevObj.release(character.name);\n              if (simState?.pushEvent) {\n                simState.pushEvent({\n                  type:      'fallback',\n                  charLabel: character.label,\n                  reason:    'plan_changed',\n                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,\n                  toLabel:   target.label,\n                });\n              }\n            }\n            character.targetObjectId = null;\n          }\n\n          // Request Phase: walk A to a tile adjacent to B.\n          // Arrival handler in Engine will start the shared talking state.\n          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));\n          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {\n            // Store pending talk so Engine knows what to do on arrival\n            character.pendingTalkTarget   = target;\n            character.pendingTalkDialogue = decision.dialogue       || null;\n            character.pendingTalkResponse = decision.targetDialogue || null;\n          }\n        }\n        break;\n      }\n    }",

{"id":"FRG-245","title":"Characters cannot overlap — add character-to-character collision","description":"## Problem

Characters walk through each other and stack on the same tile. Pathfinding (A\\*) only avoids walls and furniture. Zero character-to-character collision.

## Technical Assessment (from sub-agent)

**One session. Ship it.** \\~100-200 lines of new/modified code.

### Approach: Dynamic walkable grid + retry + deadlock escape

1. Before each A\\* call, clone the walkable grid and mark other characters' current tiles as unwalkable. Don't reserve destination tiles.
2. On path blocked (A\\* returns no path): wait 500-1000ms, then re-path. The blocker will likely have moved.
3. Deadlock breaker: if re-path fails 3 times, pick a random walkable adjacent tile, move there, then re-path to original goal.
4. Interaction/talk targeting: characters walk to adjacent tile of target. If preferred adjacent tile is blocked, try other adjacent tiles.

### Don't do

* Tile reservation systems
* Movement queues
* Priority-based yielding

### Edge cases to test

* Two characters pathing through each other
* Two characters targeting same object
* Narrow corridor crossing (1-tile wide)
* All adjacent tiles occupied (graceful fallback, not crash)

## Acceptance Criteria

* No two characters occupy the same tile
* Characters path around each other
* No deadlocks (escape valve after 3 retries)
* Existing interaction and talk systems still work","projectMilestone":{"id":"a6eb53b7-72b4-453e-9e23-aa42a629b7a4","name":"M2: Visual sim (main page)"},"priority":{"value":2,"name":"High"},"url":"https://linear.app/chills-linear/issue/FRG-245/characters-cannot-overlap-add-character-to-character-collision","gitBranchName":"devlab/frg-245-characters-cannot-overlap-add-character-to-character","createdAt":"2026-03-09T04:29:23.272Z","updatedAt":"2026-03-13T08:29:20.474Z","archivedAt":null,"completedAt":null,"dueDate":null,"slaStartedAt":null,"slaMediumRiskAt":null,"slaHighRiskAt":null,"slaBreachesAt":null,"slaType":"all","status":"Test in Progress","labels":[],"attachments":[{"id":"ff4d2ac1-5867-44ee-a605-be6dd0ecce51","title":"feat: character-to-character collision avoidance (FRG-245)","subtitle":null,"url":"https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/17"},{"id":"711bae53-7ecc-4405-8ca7-4a1710a5b31c","title":"FRG-245: add character-to-character collision avoidance","subtitle":null,"url":"https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium/pull/7"}],"documents":[],"createdBy":"Project Manager","createdById":"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7","assignee":"Project Manager","assigneeId":"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7","project":"AI Aquarium","projectId":"0385a8c7-ba5a-43a3-b223-acf4d1ad6d63","team":"Forge","teamId":"c3ef97d8-21a8-4aa7-a818-298f217864dd"}

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #112
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `src/Character.js` — Added `_failedMoveCount = 0` field; `moveTo()` now accepts an optional `walkable` grid (3rd arg, defaults to `this.walkable`) and resets `_failedMoveCount` on a successful path - `src/Engine.js` — Added `_buildDynamicWalkable(excludeChar)` which clones the static grid and marks other characters' current tiles as blocked; updated `_findAdjacentWalkable` to accept an optional walkable grid (backward compatible); updated all `moveTo` and adjacent-tile calls in `_doWander`, `_handleTalkArrival`, `_updateTalkRoute`, and `_fallbackToAlternativeObject` to use the dynamic grid; added deadlock escape valve (after 3 consecutive wander failures, step to any free adjacent tile); exposed `buildDynamicWalkable` in `simState` for AIEngine - `src/AIEngine.js` — `_applyDecision` builds a dynamic walkable grid at the start and passes it to all `moveTo` and `findAdjacentWalkable` calls (move, interact, and talk actions) ## Key Decisions - No tile reservation system — dynamic grid per A* call is the spec's prescribed approach; simpler and avoids stale reservations - `_failedMoveCount` tracks consecutive wander failures (not per-goal retries) since wander picks random tiles each time; the escape valve fires after 3 failures and steps to any adjacent free tile - Retry backoff for blocked wanders is 500–1000 ms instead of the prior 2 s, so characters respond faster once a blocker moves - `_buildDynamicWalkable` intentionally only marks current (integer) tile positions, not next-step destinations, per spec ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-245-character-collision-avoidance` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/17
